[30;1m17 | [0m[35m## Why you should use JSON-Patch[0m
[30;1m18 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m19 | [0m[35mJSON-Patch [(RFC6902)](http://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc6902) is a standard format that[0m
[30;1m20 | [0m[35mallows you to update a JSON document by sending the changes rather than the whole document.[0m
[30;1m21 | [0m[35mJSON Patch plays well with the HTTP PATCH verb (method) and REST style programming.[0m
[30;1m22 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m23 | [0m[35mMark Nottingham has a [nice blog]( http://www.mnot.net/blog/2012/09/05/patch) about it.[0m
